
=================================================================
1-SHOT
With only the questionnaire TOPIC
=================================================================

-------------------
[SAMPLE] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Leadership Effectiveness
     - Question number: 7

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "WORK_STRESS_SURVEY_001",
                "NAME": "Workplace Stress Assessment",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "WS_Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale from 1 to 5, how stressed do you feel at work on average? (1 being 'Not stressed at all' and 5 being 'Extremely stressed')",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER": "1"},
                            {"ANSWER": "2"},
                            {"ANSWER": "3"},
                            {"ANSWER": "4"},
                            {"ANSWER": "5"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "WS_Q2",
                        "NAME": "What aspects of your job do you find most stressful? (Select all that apply)",
                        "TYPE_ID": 2,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER": "Workload"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Deadlines"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Interpersonal relationships"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Work-life balance"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Lack of support from management"},
                            {"ANSWER": "(Other) Please specify:"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "WS_Q3",
                        "NAME":"How often do you feel overwhelmed by work-related stress?",
                       	"TYPE_ID" : 1,
                      	"DISPLAY_ORDER" : 3,
                      	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                        	{"ANSWER":"Daily"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"Several times a week"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"Once a week"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"A few times a month"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"Rarely"}
                      	]
                    },
                    {
                    	"CODE" :  	"WS_Q4",
                    	"NAME" :  	"Do you feel that your supervisor is understanding and supportive when you discuss your work-related stress with them?",
                    	"TYPE_ID" :   1,
                    	"DISPLAY_ORDER" :   4,
                    	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                    		{"ANSWER":"Always supportive"},

                   },

            }
        ]
    }

[SAMPLE] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146004

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146004
     - Topic: Workplace Environment
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "REMOTE_WORK_EXP_001",
                "NAME": "Remote Working Experience Survey",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "RWQ1",
                        "NAME": "How often do you work remotely?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER": "Daily"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Several times a week"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Once a week"},
                            {"ANSWER": "A few times a month"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Rarely or never"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "RWQ2",
                        "NAME": "What is your level of satisfaction with your remote work environment?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                            {"ANSWER":"Very satisfied"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Satisfied"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Neutral"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Dissatisfied"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Very dissatisfied"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE":"RWQ3",
                        "NAME":"Do you feel that you have the tools and resources needed to work effectively from home?",
                        "TYPE_ID" :1,
                        	"DISPLAY_ORDER" :3,
                        	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                        	    {"ANSWER":"Yes, completely"},
                        	    {"ANSWER":"Somewhat, but there's room for improvement"},
                        	    {"ANSWER":"No, I encounter many challenges"}
                        	]
                    },
                    {
                    	"CODE" :"RWQ4",
                    	"NAME" :"How would you rate your productivity while working remotely compared to in-office work?",
                    	"TYPE_ID" :3,
                    	"DISPLAY_ORDER" :4,
                    	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                    	    {"ANSWER":"Much higher"},
                    	    {"ANSWER":"Somewhat higher"},
                    	    {"ANSWER":"About the same"},
                    	    {"ANSWER":"Somewhat lower"},
                    	    {"ANSWER":"Much lower"}
                    	]
                    },
                    {
                    	"CODE" :"RWQ5",
                    	"NAME" :"What are the biggest challenges you face when working remotely? (Select all that apply)",
                    	"TYPE_ID" :2,
                    		"DISPLAY_ORDER" :5,
                    		"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                    		{"ANSWER":"Communication with colleagues and managers"},
                    		{"ANSWER":"Access to necessary technology or software"}, 
                    		{"ANSWER":"Distractions at home"}, 
                    		{"ANSWER":"Staying motivated"}, 
                    		{"ANSWER":"Managing work-life balance"}, 
                    		{"ANSWER":"Feeling isolated or disconnected from the team"}
                    	 ]
                    },
                    {
                     	 	 	 	
                     	 	 	 	
                     	 	 	 	
                     	 	 	 }
                ]
            }
        ]
    }
}

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100008
     - Topic: Career Path Clarity
     - Question number: 10
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Career Path Clarity
-------------------

        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:

            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.

  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.

  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

[SAMPLE] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100012
     - Topic: Onboarding Experience
     - Question number: 7

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100012
     - Topic: Employee motivation
     - Question number: 5
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Employee motivation
-------------------
-------------------

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100013
     - Topic: Employee Performance
     - Question number: 10
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Employee Performance

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

-------------------
[SAMPLE] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100032
     - Topic: Employee feedback
     - Question number: 4

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100032
     - Topic: Leadership Effectiveness
     - Question number: 8
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Leadership Effectiveness
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "LEAD_EFF_2023",
                "NAME": "Leadership Effectiveness Assessment",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "How clearly does your leader communicate the team's objectives?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER": "Not clear at all"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Somewhat unclear"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Fairly clear"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Very clear"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q2",
                        "NAME": "Does your leader provide constructive feedback?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER":"Never"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Rarely"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Sometimes"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Often"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Always"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q3",
                        "NAME":"How effective is your leader in making decisions?",
                        "TYPE_ID" : 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER" : 3,
                         "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                             {  	"ANSWER" :	"Ineffective" },
                             {  	"ANSWER" :	"Slightly effective" },
                             {  	"ANSWER" :	"Moderately effective" },
                             {  	"ANSWER" :	"Very effective" },
                             {  	"ANSWER" :	"Extremely effective"}
                         ]
                    },
                    {
                      	"CODE":"Q4",
                      	"NAME":"Rate your leader's ability to motivate the team.",
                      	"TYPE_ID ":3,
                      	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                           {  	"ANSWER":"Very poor"},
                           {  	"ANSWER":"Poor"},
                           {  	"ANSWER":"Average"},
                           {  	"ANSWER":"Good"},
                           {  	"ANSWER":"Excellent"}

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100033
     - Topic: Onboarding Experience
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Onboarding Experience
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "ONBOARDING_EXP_001",
                "NAME": "Onboarding Experience Survey",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "How clear was the information provided about the onboarding process before your first day?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER": "Very clear"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Somewhat clear"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Somewhat unclear"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Very unclear"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q2",
                        "NAME": "Did you feel welcomed by your team on your first day?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER": "Yes, very welcomed"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Somewhat welcomed"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Not very welcomed"},
                            {"ANSWER": "Not at all welcomed"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q3",
                        "NAME":"How would you rate the effectiveness of the training materials provided during onboarding?",
                       	"TYPE_ID" : 3,
                      	"DISPLAY_ORDER" : 3,
                      	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                        	{"ANSWER":"1"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"2"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"3"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"4"},
                        	{"ANSWER":"5"}
                      	]
                    },
                    {
                    	"CODE":"Q4",
                    	"NAME":"Was your role and responsibilities clearly defined during the onboarding process?",
                    	"TYPE_ID" : 1,
                    	"DISPLAY_ORDER" : 4,
                    	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                    		{"ANSWER":"Yes, very clear"},
                    		{"ANSWER":"Somewhat clear"},
                    		{"ANSWER":"Neutral"},
                    		{"ANSWER":"Not very clear"},
                    		{"ANSWER":"Not at all clear"}
                    	  ]
                  	  },
                  	  {
                  	  	  "_TF_ANSWERS":[],
                  	  	  "_TF_QUESTIONS":[],
                  	  	  "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":[],
                  	  	  "_TF_TEMPLATES":[]
                  	  }
                ]
            }
        ]
    }

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100058
     - Topic: Workload Management
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workload Management
-------------------
-------------------

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment
